       <div class="container-fluid universal-design u-design-padding py-homepage-module">
        <h2 class="module-heading">
         <span>
          Enabling transformation
         </span>
        </h2>
        <div class="d-flex flex-wrap">
         <div class="text-block col-md-6">
          <p>
           <span>
            Your edX learning experience is grounded in cutting edge cognitive science. With more than two dozen distinct learning features to help you achieve your goals, our approach follows three key principles:
           </span>
          </p>
          <h3 class="section-header">
           Experience
          </h3>
          <p>
           <span>
            Learn new knowledge and skills in a variety of ways, from engaging video lectures and dynamic graphics to data visualizations and interactive elements.
           </span>
          </p>
          <h3 class="section-header">
           Practice
          </h3>
          <p>
           <span>
            Demonstrating your knowledge is a critical part of learning. edX courses and programs provide a space to practice with quizzes, open response assessments, virtual environments, and more.
           </span>
          </p>
          <h3 class="section-header">
           Apply
          </h3>
          <p>
           <span>
            Learning on edX transforms how you think and what you can do, and translates directly into the real worldimmediately apply your new capabilities in the context of your job.
           </span>
          </p>
         </div>
         <div class="col-md-6">
          <img alt="" src="/images/stock/koosh-brain.png"/>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="edx-vision border mt-4">
        <div class="content container-fluid">
         <h2 class="h2 vision-heading mb-4">
          <span>
           Our vision
          </span>
         </h2>
         <p class="vision-description col-lg-7 p-0">
          <span>
           As a global nonprofit, we're relentlessly pursuing our vision of a world where every learner can access education to unlock their potential, without the barriers of cost or location.
          </span>
         </p>
